# Awesome Agent APIs

> A collection of APIs designed to power your agents 🤖

![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/AgentsAPI/awesome-agent-apis?style=social)
![Vistors](https://visitor-badge.laobi.icu/badge?page_id=AgentsAPI.awesome-agent-apis&title=Visitors)
![Categories](https://img.shields.io/badge/Categories-17-blue?logo=adafruit)
![API](https://img.shields.io/badge/APIs-55164-blue?logo=chainguard)
![Updated Daily](https://img.shields.io/badge/Updated-today-00c853?logo=rubocop)
![PRs Welcome](https://img.shields.io/badge/PRs-welcome-brightgreen.svg?logo=googlegemini)

## 🌟 Why Agent APIs?

Building AI agents is hard — finding the right APIs shouldn't be.

Awesome Agent APIs is a curated collection of powerful APIs that help you:

- 🤖 Build autonomous AI agents
- 🔌 Connect agents to real-world data
- ⚡ Automate complex workflows
- 🧠 Enhance LLM capabilities with external tools

👉 Stop reinventing the wheel — plug your agent into the world.

## 🧠 What Can You Build?

With these APIs, your agents can:

#### 🤖 Act like real assistants
- Search the web
- Send emails
- Manage tasks
- Interact with SaaS tools

#### 📊 Access real-time data
- Market data, trends, analytics
- News, finance, crypto
- Product & pricing data

#### 🌐 Interact with the internet
- Web scraping
- Social media automation
- Content extraction

#### 🛠️ Execute actions
- Trigger workflows
- Call external services
- Automate business logic

| [Sora Scraper](https://apify.com/lexis-solutions/sora-scraper?fpr=hs6s8) | ⭐️ 5.0 (7) | Discover AI-generated video insights from OpenAI’s Sora 2 community—extract posts, media, user profiles, comments, and engagement metrics. Perfect for trend analysis, content curation, influencer tracking, and research. Fast, reliable, and fully customizable. |
| [3d Print Generator](https://apify.com/salesmart-srl/3d-print-generator?fpr=hs6s8) | ⭐️ 4.99 (7) | AI-powered text/image to 3D model generator. Create printable STL/GLB files with mesh validation, auto-repair, and printer optimization. Supports resin (SLA) and FDM printers. Quality levels from draft to ultra. |
| [Rightmove Landregistry Full Address House Number Finder](https://apify.com/dhrumil/rightmove-landregistry-full-address-house-number-finder?fpr=hs6s8) | ⭐️ 5.0 (6) | Unlock full UK property addresses with house numbers by matching Rightmove history with Land Registry sold data. |-----|--------|-------------|
| [Web Scraper](https://apify.com/apify/web-scraper?fpr=hs6s8) | ⭐️ 4.8 (72) | Crawls arbitrary websites using a web browser and extracts structured data from web pages using a provided JavaScript function. The Actor supports both recursive crawling and lists of URLs, and automatically manages concurrency for maximum performance. |
| [Sherlock](https://apify.com/misceres/sherlock?fpr=hs6s8) | ⭐️ 4.69 (76) | 🔎 Hunt down social media accounts by username across social networks using open-source project https://github.com/sherlock-project/sherlock |
| [LinkedIn Profile Scraper + Email ✅ No Cookies](https://apify.com/harvestapi/linkedin-profile-scraper?fpr=hs6s8) | ⭐️ 4.66 (29) | Extract detailed information from LinkedIn profiles in bulk, including complete work experience, education history, skills and more. No cookies or account required. |
| [Cheerio Scraper](https://apify.com/apify/cheerio-scraper?fpr=hs6s8) | ⭐️ 4.98 (20) | Crawls websites using raw HTTP requests, parses the HTML with the Cheerio library, and extracts data from the pages using a Node.js code. Supports both recursive crawling and lists of URLs. This actor is a high-performance alternative to apify/web-scraper for websites that do not require JavaScript. |
| [LinkedIn Profile Posts Scraper (No Cookies)⚡$2 per 1k](https://apify.com/harvestapi/linkedin-profile-posts?fpr=hs6s8) | ⭐️ 4.89 (19) | Extract posts from LinkedIn profiles, including content, media, engagement, reactions, comments, and more. No cookies or account required. |
| [Puppeteer Scraper](https://apify.com/apify/puppeteer-scraper?fpr=hs6s8) | ⭐️ 4.97 (18) | Crawls websites with the headless Chrome and Puppeteer library using a provided server-side Node.js code. This crawler is an alternative to apify/web-scraper that gives you finer control over the process. Supports both recursive crawling and list of URLs. Supports login to website. |
| [Website Screenshot Generator](https://apify.com/apify/screenshot-url?fpr=hs6s8) | ⭐️ 4.38 (14) | Create a screenshot of a website based on a specified URL. The screenshot is stored as the output in a key-value store. It can be used to monitor web changes regularly after setting up the scheduler. |
| [Bing Ads Scraper](https://apify.com/lexis-solutions/bing-ads-scraper?fpr=hs6s8) | ⭐️ 5.0 (9) | Find and scrape current and past ads on Bing. Get ad copy, shown dates and locations, impressions, and more. Download and analyze data from the Microsoft Ad Library for competitive analysis. |
| [LinkedIn Post Comments Scraper (No Cookies)⚡$2 per 1k](https://apify.com/harvestapi/linkedin-post-comments?fpr=hs6s8) | ⭐️ 4.16 (11) | Extract LinkedIn post comments and comment replies in bulk, as well as comment social activities such as likes and reactions. No cookies or account required |

It is a standalone Actor server designed for testing MCP servers over Stremable HTTP. |
